Posted by Edward d'Auvergne on May 15, 2013 - 12:14:
Hi Troels,


From the Gmane archives, I can see that you are using HTML in your

emails.  Would it be possible to turn this off and use plain text for
the messages to the relax mailing lists?  This would make the archives
much cleaner, as the HTML is not handled well by some of the mailing
list archivers.  For example see:

http://thread.gmane.org/gmane.science.nmr.relax.devel/3863
http://marc.info/?l=relax-devel&m=136855598104339&w=2

Cheers,

Edward
